    4643             :     /* attempt to find a line though the point pt which is tangent to the spline */
    4644             :     /*  we return t of the tangent point on the spline (if any)           */
    4645             :     /* So the slope of the line through pt&tangent point must match slope */
    4646             :     /*  at the tangent point on the spline. Or...                         */
    4647             :     /* (pt.x-xt)/(pt.y-yt) = (dx/dt)/(dy/dt)                              */
    4648             :     /* (pt.x-xt)*(dy/dt) = (pt.y-yt)*(dx/dt)                              */
